        T.BIN_NO,
        CASE WHEN T.IO_TYPE = 'I' THEN '入库'
             WHEN T.IO_TYPE = 'O' THEN '出库'
             WHEN T.IO_TYPE = 'C' THEN '盘库修改'
        END IO_TYPE,
        T.CREATION_DATE,
        T.PALLET_NO,
        ISNULL(T1.MATER_NO,T2.MATER_NO) MATER_NO,
        ISNULL(T1.MATER_NAME,T2.MATER_NAME) MATER_NAME,
        CASE WHEN T.FINISH_FLAG IS NULL OR T.FINISH_FLAG = '_' THEN '正常'
        ELSE T.FINISH_FLAG END FINISH_FLAG
		    FROM Z50_WBS_BIN T
        LEFT JOIN WBS_PACKAGE_DATA T1 ON T1.PACKAGE_GUID = T.PACKAGE_GUID
        LEFT JOIN Z50_WBS_PACKAGE_DATA T2 ON T2.PACKAGE_GUID = T.PACKAGE_GUID

              ,T.CREATION_DATE

               T1.MATER_NAME,
               COUNT(T1.MATER_NO) AS MATERIAL_NUM,
               SUM(T1.PRODUCT_QTY) AS QTY
          FROM WBS_BIN T
         INNER JOIN WBS_PACKAGE_DATA T1 ON T1.PACKAGE_GUID =  T.PACKAGE_GUID 
       where   T.CREATION_DATE >= @param0    AND  T.CREATION_DATE <= 1+ @param1    
         GROUP BY T1.MATER_NO, T1.MATER_NAME
         ORDER BY T1.MATER_NO
参数：

@param1=2018/10/16 0:00:00

2018-10-16 15:13:49,247 [49] DEBUG IEMS.Frame.DbCI.McUIService [(null)] - IEMS.Frame.DbCI.McUIService.Select@BinStatistics
SELECT T1.MATER_NO,
               T1.MATER_NAME,
               COUNT(T1.MATER_NO) AS MATERIAL_NUM,
               SUM(T1.PRODUCT_QTY) AS QTY
          FROM WBS_BIN T
         INNER JOIN WBS_PACKAGE_DATA T1 ON T1.PACKAGE_GUID =  T.PACKAGE_GUID 
       where   T.CREATION_DATE >= @param0    AND  T.CREATION_DATE <= 1+ @param1    
         GROUP BY T1.MATER_NO, T1.MATER_NAME
         ORDER BY T1.MATER_NO
参数：
@param0=2017/10/15 0:00:00
@param1=2018/10/16 0:00:00
